<s> nay nay gentlemen two on a side are plenty says harry's patron <\s>
<s> spare the boy captain macartney and he shook harry's hand for the last time save one in his life <\s>
<s> at the bar of the tavern all the gentlemen stopped and my lord viscount said laughing to the barwoman that those cards set people sadly a quarrelling but that the dispute was over now and the parties were all going away to my lord mohun's house in bow street to drink a bottle more before going to bed <\s>
<s> a half dozen of chairs were now called and the six gentlemen stepping into them the word was privately given to the chairmen to go to leicester field where the gentlemen were set down opposite the standard tavern <\s>
<s> it was midnight and the town was abed by this time and only a few lights in the windows of the houses but the night was bright enough for the unhappy purpose which the disputants came about and so all six entered into that fatal square the chairmen standing without the railing and keeping the gate lest any persons should disturb the meeting <\s>
<s> all that happened there hath been matter of public notoriety and is recorded for warning to lawless men in the annals of our country <\s>
<s> after being engaged for not more than a couple of minutes as harry esmond thought though being occupied at the time with his own adversary's point which was active he may not have taken a good note of time a cry from the chairmen without who were smoking their pipes and leaning over the railings of the field as they watched the dim combat within announced that some catastrophe had happened which caused esmond to drop his sword and look round at which moment his enemy wounded him in the right hand <\s>
<s> but the young man did not heed this hurt much and ran up to the place where he saw his dear master was down <\s>
<s> my lord mohun was standing over him <\s>
<s> are you much hurt frank <\s>
<s> he asked in a hollow voice <\s>
<s> i believe i am a dead man my lord said from the ground <\s>
<s> no no not so says the other and i call god to witness frank esmond that i would have asked your pardon had you but given me a chance <\s>
<s> in in the first cause of our falling out i swear that no one was to blame but me and and that my lady hush <\s>
<s> says my poor lord viscount lifting himself on his elbow and speaking faintly <\s>
<s> twas a dispute about the cards the cursed cards <\s>
<s> harry my boy are you wounded too <\s>
<s> i loved thee harry and thou must watch over my little frank and and carry this little heart to my wife <\s>
<s> and here my dear lord felt in his breast for a locket he wore there and in the act fell back fainting <\s>
<s> we were all at this terrified thinking him dead but esmond and colonel westbury bade the chairmen come into the field and so my lord was carried to one mr <\s>
<s> aimes a surgeon in long acre who kept a bath and there the house was wakened up and the victim of this quarrel carried in <\s>
<s> my lord viscount was put to bed and his wound looked to by the surgeon who seemed both kind and skilful <\s>
<s> when he had looked to my lord he bandaged up harry esmond's hand who from loss of blood had fainted too in the house and may have been some time unconscious ); and when the young man came to himself you may be sure he eagerly asked what news there were of his dear patron on which the surgeon carried him to the room where the lord castlewood lay who had already sent for a priest and desired earnestly they said to speak with his kinsman <\s>
<s> he was lying on a bed very pale and ghastly with that fixed fatal look in his eyes which betokens death and faintly beckoning all the other persons away from him with his hand and crying out only harry esmond the hand fell powerless down on the coverlet as harry came forward and knelt down and kissed it <\s>
<s> thou art all but a priest harry my lord viscount gasped out with a faint smile and pressure of his cold hand <\s>
<s> are they all gone <\s>
<s> let me make thee a death bed confession <\s>

<s> twas a great chimney with glazed dutch tiles <\s>
<s> they went in at the bar of the tavern and desired a private room and wine and cards and when the drawer had brought these they began to drink and call healths and as long as the servants were in the room appeared very friendly <\s>
<s> harry esmond's plan was no other than to engage in talk with lord mohun to insult him and so get the first of the quarrel <\s>
<s> so when cards were proposed he offered to play <\s>
<s> says my lord mohun whether wishing to save harry or not choosing to try the botte de jesuite it is not to be known young gentlemen from college should not play these stakes <\s>
<s> you are too young <\s>
<s> who dares say i am too young <\s>
<s> is your lordship afraid <\s>

<s> you silly boy we don't play for groats here as you do at cambridge <\s>
<s> and harry who had no such sum in his pocket for his half year's salary was always pretty well spent before it was due fell back with rage and vexation in his heart that he had not money enough to stake <\s>
<s> i'll stake the young gentleman a crown says the lord mohun's captain <\s>
<s> i thought crowns were rather scarce with the gentlemen of the army says harry <\s>
<s> do they birch at college <\s>
<s> they birch fools says harry and they cane bullies and they fling puppies into the water <\s>
<s> faith then there's some escapes drowning says the captain who was an irishman and all the gentlemen began to laugh and made poor harry only more angry <\s>
<s> my lord mohun presently snuffed a candle <\s>
<s> it was when the drawers brought in fresh bottles and glasses and were in the room on which my lord viscount said the deuce take you mohun how damned awkward you are <\s>
<s> light the candle you drawer <\s>

<s> i'm a country gentleman says my lord viscount <\s>

<s> i fling the words in your face my lord says the other shall i send the cards too <\s>
<s> cry out colonel westbury and my lord warwick in a breath <\s>
<s> the drawers go out of the room hastily <\s>
<s> they tell the people below of the quarrel up stairs <\s>
<s> enough has been said says colonel westbury <\s>
<s> will your lordships meet to morrow morning <\s>
<s> will my lord castlewood withdraw his words <\s>
<s> asks the earl of warwick <\s>

<s> where shall the meeting be <\s>

<s> let us have chairs and go to leicester field <\s>

<s> says colonel westbury with a low bow to my lord of warwick and holland <\s>
<s> it is an honor for me says my lord with a profound congee to be matched with a gentleman who has been at mons and namur <\s>

<s> nay nay gentlemen two on a side are plenty says harry's patron <\s>
<s> spare the boy captain macartney and he shook harry's hand for the last time save one in his life <\s>
<s> at the bar of the tavern all the gentlemen stopped and my lord viscount said laughing to the barwoman that those cards set people sadly a quarrelling but that the dispute was over now and the parties were all going away to my lord mohun's house in bow street to drink a bottle more before going to bed <\s>
<s> a half dozen of chairs were now called and the six gentlemen stepping into them the word was privately given to the chairmen to go to leicester field where the gentlemen were set down opposite the standard tavern <\s>
<s> it was midnight and the town was abed by this time and only a few lights in the windows of the houses but the night was bright enough for the unhappy purpose which the disputants came about and so all six entered into that fatal square the chairmen standing without the railing and keeping the gate lest any persons should disturb the meeting <\s>
<s> all that happened there hath been matter of public notoriety and is recorded for warning to lawless men in the annals of our country <\s>
<s> after being engaged for not more than a couple of minutes as harry esmond thought though being occupied at the time with his own adversary's point which was active he may not have taken a good note of time a cry from the chairmen without who were smoking their pipes and leaning over the railings of the field as they watched the dim combat within announced that some catastrophe had happened which caused esmond to drop his sword and look round at which moment his enemy wounded him in the right hand <\s>
<s> but the young man did not heed this hurt much and ran up to the place where he saw his dear master was down <\s>
<s> my lord mohun was standing over him <\s>
<s> are you much hurt frank <\s>
<s> he asked in a hollow voice <\s>
<s> i believe i am a dead man my lord said from the ground <\s>
<s> no no not so says the other and i call god to witness frank esmond that i would have asked your pardon had you but given me a chance <\s>
<s> in in the first cause of our falling out i swear that no one was to blame but me and and that my lady hush <\s>
<s> says my poor lord viscount lifting himself on his elbow and speaking faintly <\s>
<s> twas a dispute about the cards the cursed cards <\s>
<s> harry my boy are you wounded too <\s>
<s> i loved thee harry and thou must watch over my little frank and and carry this little heart to my wife <\s>
<s> and here my dear lord felt in his breast for a locket he wore there and in the act fell back fainting <\s>
<s> we were all at this terrified thinking him dead but esmond and colonel westbury bade the chairmen come into the field and so my lord was carried to one mr <\s>
<s> aimes a surgeon in long acre who kept a bath and there the house was wakened up and the victim of this quarrel carried in <\s>
<s> my lord viscount was put to bed and his wound looked to by the surgeon who seemed both kind and skilful <\s>
<s> when he had looked to my lord he bandaged up harry esmond's hand who from loss of blood had fainted too in the house and may have been some time unconscious ); and when the young man came to himself you may be sure he eagerly asked what news there were of his dear patron on which the surgeon carried him to the room where the lord castlewood lay who had already sent for a priest and desired earnestly they said to speak with his kinsman <\s>
<s> he was lying on a bed very pale and ghastly with that fixed fatal look in his eyes which betokens death and faintly beckoning all the other persons away from him with his hand and crying out only harry esmond the hand fell powerless down on the coverlet as harry came forward and knelt down and kissed it <\s>
<s> thou art all but a priest harry my lord viscount gasped out with a faint smile and pressure of his cold hand <\s>
<s> are they all gone <\s>
<s> let me make thee a death bed confession <\s>

<s> it was midnight and the town was abed by this time and only a few lights in the windows of the houses but the night was bright enough for the unhappy purpose which the disputants came about and so all six entered into that fatal square the chairmen standing without the railing and keeping the gate lest any persons should disturb the meeting <\s>
<s> all that happened there hath been matter of public notoriety and is recorded for warning to lawless men in the annals of our country <\s>
<s> after being engaged for not more than a couple of minutes as harry esmond thought though being occupied at the time with his own adversary's point which was active he may not have taken a good note of time a cry from the chairmen without who were smoking their pipes and leaning over the railings of the field as they watched the dim combat within announced that some catastrophe had happened which caused esmond to drop his sword and look round at which moment his enemy wounded him in the right hand <\s>
<s> but the young man did not heed this hurt much and ran up to the place where he saw his dear master was down <\s>
<s> my lord mohun was standing over him <\s>
<s> are you much hurt frank <\s>
<s> he asked in a hollow voice <\s>
<s> i believe i am a dead man my lord said from the ground <\s>
<s> no no not so says the other and i call god to witness frank esmond that i would have asked your pardon had you but given me a chance <\s>
<s> in in the first cause of our falling out i swear that no one was to blame but me and and that my lady hush <\s>
<s> says my poor lord viscount lifting himself on his elbow and speaking faintly <\s>
<s> twas a dispute about the cards the cursed cards <\s>
<s> harry my boy are you wounded too <\s>
<s> i loved thee harry and thou must watch over my little frank and and carry this little heart to my wife <\s>
<s> and here my dear lord felt in his breast for a locket he wore there and in the act fell back fainting <\s>
<s> we were all at this terrified thinking him dead but esmond and colonel westbury bade the chairmen come into the field and so my lord was carried to one mr <\s>
<s> aimes a surgeon in long acre who kept a bath and there the house was wakened up and the victim of this quarrel carried in <\s>
<s> my lord viscount was put to bed and his wound looked to by the surgeon who seemed both kind and skilful <\s>
<s> when he had looked to my lord he bandaged up harry esmond's hand who from loss of blood had fainted too in the house and may have been some time unconscious ); and when the young man came to himself you may be sure he eagerly asked what news there were of his dear patron on which the surgeon carried him to the room where the lord castlewood lay who had already sent for a priest and desired earnestly they said to speak with his kinsman <\s>
<s> he was lying on a bed very pale and ghastly with that fixed fatal look in his eyes which betokens death and faintly beckoning all the other persons away from him with his hand and crying out only harry esmond the hand fell powerless down on the coverlet as harry came forward and knelt down and kissed it <\s>
<s> thou art all but a priest harry my lord viscount gasped out with a faint smile and pressure of his cold hand <\s>
<s> are they all gone <\s>
<s> let me make thee a death bed confession <\s>
<s> and with sacred death waiting as it were at the bed foot as an awful witness of his words the poor dying soul gasped out his last wishes in respect of his family his humble profession of contrition for his faults and his charity towards the world he was leaving <\s>
<s> some things he said concerned harry esmond as much as they astonished him <\s>
<s> and my lord viscount sinking visibly was in the midst of these strange confessions when the ecclesiastic for whom my lord had sent mr <\s>
<s> this gentleman had reached to no great church dignity as yet but was only preacher at st <\s>
<s> bride's drawing all the town thither by his eloquent sermons <\s>
<s> he was godson to my lord who had been pupil to his father had paid a visit to castlewood from oxford more than once and it was by his advice i think that harry esmond was sent to cambridge rather than to oxford of which place mr <\s>
<s> atterbury though a distinguished member spoke but ill <\s>
<s> our messenger found the good priest already at his books at five o'clock in the morning and he followed the man eagerly to the house where my poor lord viscount lay esmond watching him and taking his dying words from his mouth <\s>
<s> my lord hearing of mr <\s>
<s> atterbury's arrival and squeezing esmond's hand asked to be alone with the priest and esmond left them there for this solemn interview <\s>
<s> you may be sure that his own prayers and grief accompanied that dying benefactor <\s>
<s> my lord had said to him that which confounded the young man informed him of a secret which greatly concerned him <\s>
<s> indeed after hearing it he had had good cause for doubt and dismay for mental anguish as well as resolution <\s>
<s> while the colloquy between mr <\s>
<s> atterbury and his dying penitent took place within an immense contest of perplexity was agitating lord castlewood's young companion <\s>
<s> at the end of an hour it may be more mr <\s>
<s> atterbury came out of the room looking very hard at esmond and holding a paper <\s>
<s> he is on the brink of god's awful judgment the priest whispered <\s>
<s> he has made his breast clean to me <\s>
<s> he forgives and believes and makes restitution <\s>
<s> shall it be in public <\s>
<s> shall we call a witness to sign it <\s>
<s> god knows sobbed out the young man my dearest lord has only done me kindness all his life <\s>
<s> the priest put the paper into esmond's hand <\s>
<s> he looked at it <\s>
<s> it swam before his eyes <\s>
<s> tis a confession he said <\s>
<s> tis as you please said mr <\s>
<s> there was a fire in the room where the cloths were drying for the baths and there lay a heap in a corner saturated with the blood of my dear lord's body <\s>
<s> esmond went to the fire and threw the paper into it <\s>
<s> twas a great chimney with glazed dutch tiles <\s>
<s> they went in at the bar of the tavern and desired a private room and wine and cards and when the drawer had brought these they began to drink and call healths and as long as the servants were in the room appeared very friendly <\s>
<s> harry esmond's plan was no other than to engage in talk with lord mohun to insult him and so get the first of the quarrel <\s>
<s> so when cards were proposed he offered to play <\s>
<s> says my lord mohun whether wishing to save harry or not choosing to try the botte de jesuite it is not to be known young gentlemen from college should not play these stakes <\s>
<s> you are too young <\s>
<s> who dares say i am too young <\s>
<s> is your lordship afraid <\s>
<s> but my good lord viscount saw the move i'll play you for ten moidores mohun says he <\s>
<s> you silly boy we don't play for groats here as you do at cambridge <\s>
<s> and harry who had no such sum in his pocket for his half year's salary was always pretty well spent before it was due fell back with rage and vexation in his heart that he had not money enough to stake <\s>
<s> i'll stake the young gentleman a crown says the lord mohun's captain <\s>
<s> i thought crowns were rather scarce with the gentlemen of the army says harry <\s>
<s> do they birch at college <\s>
<s> they birch fools says harry and they cane bullies and they fling puppies into the water <\s>
<s> faith then there's some escapes drowning says the captain who was an irishman and all the gentlemen began to laugh and made poor harry only more angry <\s>
<s> my lord mohun presently snuffed a candle <\s>
<s> it was when the drawers brought in fresh bottles and glasses and were in the room on which my lord viscount said the deuce take you mohun how damned awkward you are <\s>
<s> light the candle you drawer <\s>
<s> damned awkward is a damned awkward expression my lord says the other <\s>
<s> town gentlemen don't use such words or ask pardon if they do <\s>
<s> i'm a country gentleman says my lord viscount <\s>
<s> i see it by your manner says my lord mohun <\s>
<s> no man shall say damned awkward to me <\s>
<s> i fling the words in your face my lord says the other shall i send the cards too <\s>
<s> cry out colonel westbury and my lord warwick in a breath <\s>
<s> the drawers go out of the room hastily <\s>
<s> they tell the people below of the quarrel up stairs <\s>
<s> enough has been said says colonel westbury <\s>
<s> will your lordships meet to morrow morning <\s>
<s> will my lord castlewood withdraw his words <\s>
<s> asks the earl of warwick <\s>
<s> my lord castlewood will be first says colonel westbury <\s>
<s> then we have nothing for it <\s>
<s> take notice gentlemen there have been outrageous words reparation asked and refused <\s>
<s> and refused says my lord castlewood putting on his hat <\s>
<s> where shall the meeting be <\s>
<s> since my lord refuses me satisfaction which i deeply regret there is no time so good as now says my lord mohun <\s>
<s> let us have chairs and go to leicester field <\s>
<s> are your lordship and i to have the honor of exchanging a pass or two <\s>
<s> says colonel westbury with a low bow to my lord of warwick and holland <\s>
<s> it is an honor for me says my lord with a profound congee to be matched with a gentleman who has been at mons and namur <\s>

<s> says colonel westbury with a low bow to my lord of warwick and holland <\s>
<s> it is an honor for me says my lord with a profound congee to be matched with a gentleman who has been at mons and namur <\s>

<s> nay nay gentlemen two on a side are plenty says harry's patron <\s>

<s> at the bar of the tavern all the gentlemen stopped and my lord viscount said laughing to the barwoman that those cards set people sadly a quarrelling but that the dispute was over now and the parties were all going away to my lord mohun's house in bow street to drink a bottle more before going to bed <\s>
<s> a half dozen of chairs were now called and the six gentlemen stepping into them the word was privately given to the chairmen to go to leicester field where the gentlemen were set down opposite the standard tavern <\s>
<s> it was midnight and the town was abed by this time and only a few lights in the windows of the houses but the night was bright enough for the unhappy purpose which the disputants came about and so all six entered into that fatal square the chairmen standing without the railing and keeping the gate lest any persons should disturb the meeting <\s>
<s> all that happened there hath been matter of public notoriety and is recorded for warning to lawless men in the annals of our country <\s>
<s> after being engaged for not more than a couple of minutes as harry esmond thought though being occupied at the time with his own adversary's point which was active he may not have taken a good note of time a cry from the chairmen without who were smoking their pipes and leaning over the railings of the field as they watched the dim combat within announced that some catastrophe had happened which caused esmond to drop his sword and look round at which moment his enemy wounded him in the right hand <\s>
<s> but the young man did not heed this hurt much and ran up to the place where he saw his dear master was down <\s>
<s> my lord mohun was standing over him <\s>
<s> are you much hurt frank <\s>
<s> he asked in a hollow voice <\s>
<s> i believe i am a dead man my lord said from the ground <\s>
<s> no no not so says the other and i call god to witness frank esmond that i would have asked your pardon had you but given me a chance <\s>
<s> in in the first cause of our falling out i swear that no one was to blame but me and and that my lady hush <\s>
<s> says my poor lord viscount lifting himself on his elbow and speaking faintly <\s>
<s> twas a dispute about the cards the cursed cards <\s>
<s> harry my boy are you wounded too <\s>
<s> i loved thee harry and thou must watch over my little frank and and carry this little heart to my wife <\s>
<s> and here my dear lord felt in his breast for a locket he wore there and in the act fell back fainting <\s>
<s> we were all at this terrified thinking him dead but esmond and colonel westbury bade the chairmen come into the field and so my lord was carried to one mr <\s>
<s> aimes a surgeon in long acre who kept a bath and there the house was wakened up and the victim of this quarrel carried in <\s>
<s> my lord viscount was put to bed and his wound looked to by the surgeon who seemed both kind and skilful <\s>
<s> when he had looked to my lord he bandaged up harry esmond's hand who from loss of blood had fainted too in the house and may have been some time unconscious ); and when the young man came to himself you may be sure he eagerly asked what news there were of his dear patron on which the surgeon carried him to the room where the lord castlewood lay who had already sent for a priest and desired earnestly they said to speak with his kinsman <\s>
<s> he was lying on a bed very pale and ghastly with that fixed fatal look in his eyes which betokens death and faintly beckoning all the other persons away from him with his hand and crying out only harry esmond the hand fell powerless down on the coverlet as harry came forward and knelt down and kissed it <\s>
<s> thou art all but a priest harry my lord viscount gasped out with a faint smile and pressure of his cold hand <\s>
<s> are they all gone <\s>
<s> let me make thee a death bed confession <\s>
<s> and with sacred death waiting as it were at the bed foot as an awful witness of his words the poor dying soul gasped out his last wishes in respect of his family his humble profession of contrition for his faults and his charity towards the world he was leaving <\s>
